[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mxhtmlContentHandler.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTR[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:                    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell : row[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotalRows == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:                            firstRowColCount++;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:                        cell = [0m[1;35mcellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Identify and isolate the expensive loops**  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `[0m[1;35mCellFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, once a matching `&fraction_format` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirective is found, the code computes two nested loops whose bounds are driven by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`denomLength` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe number of ‘#’ characters specified by the user[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. For large [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`denomLength` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m per the regex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, these loops become effectively unbounded [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand cause the parser to hang.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Introduce a safe upper bound for `denomLength`**  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Define a new constant in `CellFormatter`:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Maximum number of fractional digits we will attempt to brute‐force[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final int MAX_DENOM_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This limit yields at most ~[0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m1e6[0m[39m loop iterations in the worst [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase—well within a sub‐second execution bound.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Short-circuit or degrade gracefully on oversized directives**  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Immediately after parsing out the user-specified denominator format string, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsert a guard:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     String denomFormat = [0m[1;35mfractionFormatMatcher.group[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDENOM_GROUP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int denomLength = [0m[1;35mdenomFormat.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdenomLength > MAX_DENOM_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Defer to the raw decimal or skip fraction formatting altogether[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return cell;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Here, `DENOM_GROUP` is the capturing‐group index for the denominator portion of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe regex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe “[0m[35m/[0m[39m#[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m” group[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. If `denomLength` exceeds `MAX_DENOM_LENGTH`, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod returns the original cell text unchanged, effectively bypassing the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpensive loops.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserve existing functionality for typical uses**  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For small `denomLength` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m≤[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the fraction‐finding loops execute as before, so[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting CSVs with modest fraction precision are handled normally.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For malformed or overly large fraction‐format directives, users will simply [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msee the unformatted decimal string, not an error or exception.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Implement this change in the initial codebase**  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edit only `CellFormatter.java`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not modify the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TextAndCSVParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or any test code. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter the CSV parsing loop in `TextAndCSVParser`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Rationale and side‐effect mitigation**  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - *Optimality*: This patch directly limits the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39munbounded iteration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout rewriting core logic.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - *Compatibility*: Small fractions and legacy behavior remain intact; no new [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies are introduced.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - *Side effects*: Extremely large fraction‐format requests now produce the raw [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcell text rather than a rational approximation. This is acceptable as a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDoS‐protection tradeoff; real‐world spreadsheets rarely require >[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m digits of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenominator precision.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - *Future enhancement*: If richer fraction approximation is desired, replace the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrute‐force double loops with a continued‐fraction algorithm [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in digit count[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand remove `MAX_DENOM_LENGTH` once performance and correctness are assured.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Validation**  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests for CSV parsing to ensure no regressions.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a quick performance test [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot in the fuzzer harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeding in a cell [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlike `[0m[1;36m12.345[0m[39m&[0m[33mfraction_format[0m[39m=[0m[32m"########"[0m[35m/[0m[39m########"`. Verify the method returns [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm the fuzzer no longer times out on crafted inputs exceeding the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthreshold.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
